Conversation/Tutorial/Line00001,在《星海爭霸II》，你是以率領部隊的指揮官角度去俯瞰戰場，利用滑鼠去控制你的視野，以及對你控制的單位下達命令。 /// In StarCraft II you view the battle from above as the commander of an army. You use your mouse to control your view of the battlefield and give instructions to the units under your command.=655
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00002,畫面左下方的為小地圖，可以讓你查看戰場各個角落發生的大小事情。 /// In the lower left of your screen is a minimap that allows you to see what is happening all over the battlefield.=656
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00003,畫面右下方的為指令欄，你可以使用指令欄來對選定的單位下達命令。 /// In the lower right of your screen you can find the command card. The command card is used to issue orders to selected units.=657
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00004,畫面正下方的為單位資訊面板，可顯示當前選定的單位或建築物資訊。 /// The lower middle of your screen is the unit information panel. This shows information about the units or structures you have selected.=658
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00006,想改變你的視野，將滑鼠游標移至畫面邊緣，當游標到達畫面邊緣時，畫面視野便會朝那個方向移動。 /// To change your view, move the mouse cursor to the edge of the screen. When your mouse touches the edge of the screen, your view will slide in that direction.=659
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00007,你也可以利用小地圖將視野迅速轉移至戰場上任意地點，只要以滑鼠左鍵點擊地圖後便會跳到該處。 /// You can also use the minimap to shift your view to any part of the battlefield. Simply left-click on the minimap to jump to a new location.=660
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00008,你點選了一個單位，右鍵點擊地面便可命令該單位移動到那。 /// Now that you have a unit selected, right-click on the ground to order the unit to move somewhere.=661
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00009,在移動你的單位之前，先選擇要下達命令的單位，以滑鼠左鍵點擊該單位即可。 /// To move a unit you must first select it. Use your mouse and left-click on the unit to select it.=662
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00010,做得很好，指揮官。 /// Well done commander.=663
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00011,想攻擊敵人，選好指定的單位後再右鍵點擊攻擊即可。 /// To attack an enemy, select your units and right-click on the enemy.=664
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00012,在攻擊的時候，將滑鼠游標移到敵人身上，便會看到代表生命值的生命條。當單位生命降至零就會被消滅，也可以將滑鼠游標移至我方單位身上查看該單位生命值。 /// During the attack, you can mouse over the enemy to see a bar representing their life. A unit is destroyed when its hit-points reach zero. You can also mouse over your own units to keep an eye on their life bars.=665
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00014,想下達「警戒式移動」命令，先點選單位，然後再點擊指令欄上的「攻擊」按鈕，接著再左鍵點擊某處指定部隊移動的地點。 /// To make an attack-move command, left-click on the attack button from the command card while your units are selected, and then left-click on the ground where you want your units to go.=666
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00015,若要建造一個新的人類建築，先按左鍵點選一台太空工程車。 /// To create a new terran structure, first select an SCV by left-clicking.=667
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00016,現在，按左鍵點選畫面右下方的「建造建築」按鈕。 /// Now left-click the "Build Structure" button in the lower right of your screen.=668
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00017,左鍵點擊想要建造的建築，再以左鍵點擊地面的任何地方來命令太空工程車前往放置該新建築。工程車會前往你所選擇的地點來建造該建築。 /// Left-click on the structure you want to build and then left-click anywhere on the ground to order the SCV to place the new structure. The SCV will move to your chosen location, and build the structure there.=669
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00018,指揮中心不能建在太靠近晶礦的地方或者是其他特殊的地形。按左鍵放置指揮中心時，請放置在覆蓋圖全為綠色的地方。 /// The Command Center cannot be constructed too close to minerals. When placing the Command Center look for the overlay to be completely green before left-clicking.=670
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00019,太空工程車是用來採集資源的主要工具。選取太空工程車後，按右鍵點選一個晶礦場以開始採集資源。 /// SCVs are your primary means of collecting resources. While your SCV is selected, right-click a mineral field to begin collecting resources.=671
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00020,太空工程車將會開始採集晶礦並將採到的晶礦送回最近的指揮中心。 /// Your SCV will start harvesting minerals and dropping them off at the closest Command Center.=672
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00021,你可以在指揮中心訓練更多的太空工程車好加快晶礦採集速度。 /// You can train more SCVs from the Command Center to gather minerals faster.=673
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00022,太空工程車會一直進行採集作業，直到你下達其他命令為止。 /// Your SCV will continue harvesting until you order it to do something else.=674
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00023,做得好，指揮官。採集晶礦是人類種族戰略重要的一環。 /// Well done commander. Harvesting minerals is central to any terran strategy.=675
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00024,若要訓練新的單位，你必須先選取訓練該單位的建築，例如選取兵營來查看你能訓練哪些單位。那些單位將會出現在畫面右下方的指令欄中。 /// To create new units, you must first select a structure that trains units. Select a Barracks to see what units you can train from it. Those units will appear in the command card in the lower right of your screen.=676
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00025,按左鍵點擊指令欄中的「陸戰隊」來命令兵營開始訓練該單位。當單位訓練完成時會出現在兵營的旁邊。 /// Left-click on the "Marine" button in the command card to order the Barracks to begin training that unit. Once the unit is complete, it will appear next to the Barracks.=677
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00026,你可以一次將複數單位排入佇列之中。再次點選這個按鈕便可將另一個陸戰隊加入佇列。 /// You can queue multiple units at the same time. Simply click on the button again to add another Marine to the queue.=678
